Loft with a QUEEN-size natural latex foam bed, beautiful linens, luxury towels, two leather armchairs, dining table and chairs, smart 40” HDTV with Netflix, High speed WiFi. Kitchen has full-size fridge, walk-in shower. Sleeps two comfortably. Note: low ceiling in loft. Guest house is on the Beverly Glen Blvd which can be quite busy at certain time of the day! Apartment is professionally CLEANED for each guest. Please be sure to check out the online guide book for great suggestions on fun LA things to do and see. We LOVE our place and take care of it like it's our baby and we expect you to as well! :) Please email some info on yourself, guests and plans for your trip. Looking forward to having you!

The guest house is 10 minutes walking distance to the Beverly Glen Cleaner's pick up and drop off laundry, Beverly Glen country store and only short drive to the Beverly Glen Circle, the secret hideaway of the stars and entertainment execs, complete with Starbucks, Japanese, Chinese, Italian, American and the Herb Alpert's famous Vibrato Grill and Lounge, just 3 lights up. Beverly Glen has been an haven of artists such as Henry Miller, who started "The Air-Conditioned Nightmare" here, and David Crosby who wrote many songs in the Glen including "Triad" and "Almost Cut My Hair".                       <div data-reactid="1333">
                       Ultimate VIEW estate in Bel Air Los Angeles, reminiscent of a 5-Star hotel after recent $1mm renovation. Forget Beverly Hills; stay in uber prestigious Bel Air, home to the world's most expensive giga-mansions, superstars, world leaders and Fortune 100 CEOs.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1334">
                       Home is located in Bel Air, Los Angeles, the neighborhood known for having the most expensive estates in the U.S. Set in a sanctuary-like neighborhood with hills and canyons behind exclusives gates, huge hillside mansions on the scenic drive to the home transport you to the French and Italian riviera. The local Bel Air Country Club provides a tranquil and elegant backdrop and the world-famous Hotel Bel Air is just down the street. Nearby hotels such as Hotel Bel Air and the Beverly Hills Hotel routinely charge $1,000 per night just for a standard room. This home is a luxurious, 5,000 sf multi-level home furnished to the nines with new furniture and marble and hardwood finishes throughout the home. There are four expansive decks, all with lounging areas and 180 degree views from the canyons to Hollywood Hills, to downtown LA skyline, to city lights, to Catalina Island to the pacific ocean. Relax on the deck for breakfast, afternoon tea, or a romantic dinner followed by a soak in the jacuzzi. Whether you want to do yoga on the deck in the morning amid luscious canyons and clean air, or sunbathe in the afternoon sunlight with friends, this home is appropriate for vacationing singles, on-the-road executives, reuniting longtime friends, and large family getaways alike. Being equidistant to EVERYTHING in LA, this home is centrally located: 5 minutes to Beverly Hills and 10 minutes to Rodeo Drive, 7 minutes to the Getty Museum, 7 minutes to nightlife on Sunset Boulevard, 15 minutes to Santa Monica and the beach, 15 minutes to Pacific Palisades and hiking trails, 20 minutes to Hollywood, 20 minutes to Downtown LA, 20 minutes to Universal Studios, 30 minutes to Malibu, 45 minutes to Disneyland, 45 minutes to Newport Beach and Orange County, and so much more!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1335">
                       Bel Air and adjacent Holmby Hills, along with Beverly Hills, are collectively known as "The Platinum Triangle" in Los Angeles, for its reputation of being the most exclusive real estate in virtually all of California, and possibly, the United States. The neighborhood is known to be home to sprawling giga-mansions (beyond "mega-mansions") up to 100,000 sf. The most expensive home currently for sale IN THE WORLD (at $250 million USD) is located right here in Bel Air. Bel Air is conveniently located right in the middle of all the action, near UCLA and beaches, and a hop away from nearby Hollywood Hills, yet it feels like you're in your own oasis (in a different country) once you enter the gates that surround the affluent enclave. Security guards routinely patrol the neighborhood for your safety and comfort.
                      </div>
